################################################################################################################################################
# This file and the two others are used to improve the French Translation of Millennium Dawn mod                                               #
# They are based on vanilla HOI4 French Translator's work, Nicolas Fouqué                                                                      #
# NOTE : This file depends on localisation/0_FR_loc.yml                                                                                        #
#                                                                                                                                              #
# French Translation extra files are the following:                                                                                            #
# - common/scripted_triggers/00_scripted_triggers_FR_loc.txt     Used for nation articles (Ex: LA France, LES États-Unis, ... )                #
# - common/scripted_localisation/00_scripted_localisation_FR_loc.txt     Used for nation adjectives and inhabitants (from 0_FR_loc.yml file)   #
# - localisation/0_FR_loc.yml     Used for nation adjectives and inhabitants (00_scripted_localisation_FR_loc.txt is needed to make them work) #
################################################################################################################################################

### Ex. "They invaded Japan/Iran/Italy/France/USA/Cuba." => "Ils ont envahi [le] Japon/[l']Iran/[l']Italie/[la] France/[les] États-Unis/Cuba." (lower case / minuscule)

	name = GetLeLaLNP

	name = GetIdeologie

		trigger = { has_government = fascism }

		trigger = { has_government = communism }
		localization_key = FRLOC_COMMUNISME
	}

		trigger = { has_government = democratic }
		localization_key = FRLOC_DEMOCRATIE
	}
	text = {
		trigger = { has_government = neutrality }
		localization_key = FRLOC_NEUTRALITE
	}
	text = {
		trigger = { has_government = nationalist }
		localization_key = FRLOC_NATIONALISTE
	}
}

	text = {

	}
}
